(NYSE&#58; MPC) today reported net income attributable to MPC of $845 million, or $1.49 per diluted share, for the first quarter of 2022, compared with a net loss of $242 million, or $(0.37) per diluted share, for the first quarter of 2021. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, and amortization (adjusted EBITDA) was $2.6 billion in the first quarter of 2022, compared with $1.6 billion for the first quarter of 2021. The first quarter of 2021 includes $332 million of adjusted EBITDA from discontinued operations.</font></div><div id="ib872143a3f8f492391fb4a3a3f63f9be_4"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;MPC first quarter results reflect our team&#8217;s ability to execute on our strategic pillars in these market conditions,&#8221; said President and Chief Executive Officer Michael J. Hennigan. &#8220;This quarter we advanced our low carbon strategy with the announcement of our intent to form a joint venture with Neste at our Martinez Renewable Fuels Facility and a 15% Scope 3 absolute GHG emission reduction target. We have now completed approximately $8 billion of MPC share repurchases since the inception of our $10 billion return of capital program.&#8221; </font></div><div style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Refining &#38; Marketing (R&#38;M)</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Segment adjusted EBITDA was $1.4 billion in the first quarter of 2022, versus $23 million for the first quarter of 2021. Segment adjusted EBITDA excludes refining planned turnaround costs, which totaled $145 million in the first quarter of 2022 and $112 million in the first quarter of 2021. First-quarter 2021 segment adjusted EBITDA also excludes winter storm effects of $31 million.</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> The increase in R&#38;M EBITDA was driven by higher margins and throughput in all regions.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">R&#38;M margin was $15.31 per barrel for the first quarter of 2022, versus $10.16 pe</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">r barrel for the first quarter of 2021. Crude capacity utilization was 91%, resulting in total throughput of 2.8 million barrels per day for the first quarter of 2022. This compares to crude capacity utilization of 83% for the first quarter of 2021, which resulted in total throughput of 2.6 million barrels per day.</font></div><div id="ib872143a3f8f492391fb4a3a3f63f9be_19"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Midstream</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Segment adjusted EBITDA was $1.4 billion in the first quarter of 2022, versus $1.3 billion for the first quarter of 2021. First-quarter 2021 segment adjusted </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">EBITDA excludes winter storm effects of $16 million.</font></div><div id="ib872143a3f8f492391fb4a3a3f63f9be_22"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Corporate and Items Not Allocated</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Corporate expenses totaled $151 million in the first quarter of 2022, compared with $157 million in the first quarter of 2021.</font><font style="color:#ee2724;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">2</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div></div><div id="ib872143a3f8f492391fb4a3a3f63f9be_25"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Speedway </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">This business was sold on May 14, 2021. Historic results are reported as discontinued operations. </font></div><div id="ib872143a3f8f492391fb4a3a3f63f9be_28"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Financial Position and Liquidity </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">As of March 31, 2022, MPC had $10.6 billion of cash, cash equivalents, and short-term investments. There were no borrowings outstanding under the company&#8217;s $5 billion five-year bank revolving credit facility. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">MPC debt at the end of the first quarter of 2022 totaled $7.0 billion, excluding MPLX debt. MPC&#8217;s debt-to-capital ratio, excluding MPLX debt, was 22% at the end of the first quarter of 2022.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On March 14, 2022, MPLX issued $1.5 billion aggregate principal amount of 4.950% senior notes due March 2052.  As of March 31, 2022, MPLX had repaid approximately $1.1 billion of the amount outstanding under the intercompany loan with MPC.</font></div><div id="ib872143a3f8f492391fb4a3a3f63f9be_31"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Strategic and Operations Update</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Since the last earnings call, the company has repurchased approximately $2.5 billion of company shares, and has completed, as of April 30, 2022, approximately 80% of the $10 billion repurchase program. The company has approximately $7 billion remaining under its share repurchase authorizations. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">MPC announced it has entered into definitive agreements to form a joint venture with Neste for Marathon&#8217;s Martinez renewable fuels project. The partnership will be structured as a 50&#47;50 joint venture with Neste expected to contribute a total of $1 billion, inclusive of half of the total estimated development costs. MPC will continue to manage project execution and operate the facility once construction is complete. The closing of the joint venture is subject to customary closing conditions and regulatory approvals, including obtaining the necessary permits, which depend upon certification of a final Environmental Impact Report. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Martinez facility is currently targeted to have a production capacity of 260 million gallons per year of renewable diesel in the second half of 2022, with pretreatment capabilities to come online in 2023. The facility is expected to be capable of producing 730 million gallons per year by the end of 2023. The expected and targeted timelines for achieving the production capacities outlined above are dependent upon the timing of obtaining the necessary permits to operate the facility. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On February 14, 2022, MPC established a 2030 target to reduce absolute Scope 3 &#8211; Category 11 greenhouse gas (GHG) emissions by 15% below 2019 levels. The new Scope 3 target further enhances MPC's GHG disclosures and is part of the company&#8217;s commitment to continuously improve its environmental performance while meeting society's energy needs sustainably. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Midstream segment remains focused on executing the strategic priorities of strict capital discipline, embedding a low cost culture, and optimizing the portfolio. MPLX continues to evaluate opportunities to expand its logistics to meet the needs of today and participate in an energy-diverse future. </font></div><div The company operates the nation&#8217;s largest refining system. MPC&#8217;s marketing system includes branded locations across the United States, including Marathon brand retail outlets. MPC also owns the general partner and majority limited partner interest in MPLX LP, a midstream company that owns and operates gathering, processing, and fractionation assets, as well as crude oil and light product transportation and logistics infrastructure. More information is available at www.marathonpetroleum.com.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Investor Relations Contacts&#58; style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Management uses certain financial measures to evaluate our operating performance that are calculated and presented on the basis of methodologies other than in accordance with GAAP. We believe these non-GAAP financial measures are useful to investors and analysts to assess our ongoing financial performance because, when reconciled to their most comparable GAAP financial measures, they provide improved comparability between periods through the exclusion of certain items that we believe are not indicative of our core operating performance and that may obscure our underlying business results and trends. These measures should not be considered a substitute for, or superior to, measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP, and our calculations thereof may not be comparable to similarly titled measures reported by other companies. The non-GAAP financial measures we use are as follows&#58;</font></div><div id="ib872143a3f8f492391fb4a3a3f63f9be_85"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Adjusted Net Income Attributable to MPC</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted net income attributable to MPC is defined as net income attributable to MPC excluding the items in the table below, along with their related income tax effect. For the first quarter of 2021 presented, we applied a combined federal and state statutory tax rate of 24% to the adjusted pre-tax income or loss. We have excluded these items because we believe that they are not indicative of our core operating performance and that their exclusion results in an important measure of our ongoing financial performance to better assess our underlying business results and trends. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;padding-right:6.75pt"><font
